{'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="courses/css/lesson9.html">\n<!DOCTYPE html>\n<html lang="en">\n<head>\n    <meta charset="UTF-8">\n    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">\n    <title>Lesson 9: Responsive Design - Learner</title>\n    <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../css/styles.css">\n</head>\n<body>\n    <header>\n        <div class="header-content">\n            <h1 class="logo">Learner</h1>\n            <nav>\n                <a href="../../index.html">Home</a>\n                <a href="index.html">CSS Course</a>\n            </nav>\n        </div>\n    </header>\n    \n    <main>\n        <div class="lesson-header">\n            <span class="lesson-badge">Pro Level</span>\n            <h1>Lesson 9: Responsive Design</h1>\n            <p>Create websites that work on all screen sizes</p>\n            <div class="progress-bar">\n                <div class="progress" style="width: 75%;"></div>\n            </div>\n            <span class="progress-text">Lesson 9 of 12</span>\n        </div>\n        \n        <div class="lesson-content">\n            <section class="intro">\n                <h2>What is Responsive Design?</h2>\n                <p>Responsive web design ensures your website looks and works well on all devices — from tiny phones to large desktop monitors. With mobile traffic exceeding desktop, responsive design is essential. The key ingredients are fluid layouts, flexible images, media queries, and a mobile-first approach.</p>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>1. The Viewport Meta Tag</h2>\n                <p>Essential for mobile browsers to render pages correctly.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Always include this in your HTML head */\n&lt;meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0"&gt;\n\n/* What it does:\n   - width=device-width: Page width matches device width\n   - initial-scale=1.0: Start at 100% zoom (no zooming)\n\n/* Without this tag:\n   - Mobile browsers assume desktop width (980px)\n   - Everything is tiny and requires zooming\n   - User experience is poor\n\n/* Additional options */\n&lt;meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0, maximum-scale=5.0"&gt;\n\n/* Be careful with: */\n/* user-scalable=no - Prevents zooming (accessibility issue!) */\n/* maximum-scale=1 - Prevents zooming (accessibility issue!) */</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <strong>Accessibility note:</strong> Never disable user zooming. People with low vision need to zoom to read content.\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>2. Media Queries</h2>\n                <p>Media queries apply different styles based on device characteristics.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Basic media query syntax */\n@media (condition) {\n  /* Styles that apply when condition is true */\n}\n\n/* Common breakpoint: screen width */\n@media (max-width: 768px) {\n  /* Styles for screens 768px and narrower */\n  .container {\n    padding: 10px;\n  }\n}\n\n@media (min-width: 769px) {\n  /* Styles for screens wider than 768px */\n  .container {\n    padding: 20px;\n  }\n}\n\n/* Multiple conditions */\n@media (min-width: 768px) and (max-width: 1024px) {\n  /* Styles for tablets */\n}\n\n/* Orientation */\n@media (orientation: landscape) {\n  /* Styles for landscape orientation */\n}\n\n@media (orientation: portrait) {\n  /* Styles for portrait orientation */\n}\n\n/* Screen type */\n@media screen {\n  /* Only for screens (not print) */\n}\n\n@media print {\n  /* Only for printing */\n}\n\n/* Combining with not */\n@media not print {\n  /* Everything except print */\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="explanation">\n                    <strong>Common breakpoints:</strong>\n                    <ul>\n                        <li><code>max-width: 576px</code> — Extra small phones</li>\n                        <li><code>max-width: 768px</code> — Tablets portrait</li>\n                        <li><code>max-width: 992px</code> — Tablets landscape, small laptops</li>\n                        <li><code>max-width: 1200px</code> — Desktops</li>\n                        <li><code>min-width: 1201px</code> — Large desktops</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>3. Mobile-First Approach</h2>\n                <p>Start with mobile styles, then add complexity for larger screens.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Mobile-first: Base styles for mobile */\n.container {\n  width: 100%;\n  padding: 15px;\n}\n\n/* Progressive enhancement for larger screens */\n@media (min-width: 576px) {\n  .container {\n    max-width: 540px;\n    margin: 0 auto;\n  }\n}\n\n@media (min-width: 768px) {\n  .container {\n    max-width: 720px;\n    padding: 20px;\n  }\n}\n\n@media (min-width: 992px) {\n  .container {\n    max-width: 960px;\n  }\n}\n\n@media (min-width: 1200px) {\n  .container {\n    max-width: 1140px;\n  }\n}\n\n/* Benefits of mobile-first:\n   ✓ Simpler CSS (less code)\n   ✓ Better performance on mobile\n   ✓ Forces focus on essential content\n   ✓ Uses min-width queries (more intuitive)\n*/\n\n/* Desktop-first approach (not recommended) */\n.container {\n  max-width: 1140px;\n}\n\n@media (max-width: 1199px) {\n  .container {\n    max-width: 960px;\n  }\n}\n/* More overrides needed, harder to maintain */</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <strong>Why mobile-first:</strong> Mobile styles are simpler and more constrained. Adding complexity for larger screens is easier than removing it for smaller screens.\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>4. Fluid Layouts</h2>\n                <p>Use relative units so layouts adapt to any screen size.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Percentages for widths */\n.container {\n  width: 90%;           /* 90% of parent */\n  max-width: 1200px;    /* But never wider than 1200px */\n  margin: 0 auto;       /* Center it */\n}\n\n/* Fluid grid */\n.column {\n  width: 33.333%;       /* One third */\n}\n\n/* Two columns: 25% + 75% */\n.sidebar {\n  width: 25%;\n}\n\n.main {\n  width: 75%;\n}\n\n/* Fluid typography with clamp() */\nh1 {\n  /* min, preferred, max */\n  font-size: clamp(1.5rem, 4vw, 3rem);\n  /* Minimum: 1.5rem\n     Preferred: 4% of viewport width\n     Maximum: 3rem */\n}\n\n/* Fluid padding */\n.section {\n  padding: clamp(1rem, 5vw, 3rem);\n}\n\n/* Fluid gap */\n.grid {\n  display: grid;\n  gap: clamp(1rem, 3vw, 2rem);\n}\n\n/* Viewport-based units */\n.hero {\n  height: 100vh;        /* Full viewport height */\n  min-height: 50vh;     /* At least half viewport */\n}\n\n.sidebar {\n  width: 20vw;          /* 20% of viewport width */\n}\n\n.font-size {\n  font-size: 2vmin;     /* 2% of smaller viewport dimension */\n  font-size: 2vmax;     /* 2% of larger viewport dimension */\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="explanation">\n                    <strong>Viewport units:</strong>\n                    <ul>\n                        <li><code>vw</code> — 1% of viewport width</li>\n                        <li><code>vh</code> — 1% of viewport height</li>\n                        <li><code>vmin</code> — 1% of smaller dimension</li>\n                        <li><code>vmax</code> — 1% of larger dimension</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>5. Flexible Images</h2>\n                <p>Make images responsive so they never overflow their containers.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Basic responsive image */\nimg {\n  max-width: 100%;      /* Never wider than container */\n  height: auto;         /* Maintain aspect ratio */\n}\n\n/* Images in content */\n.content img {\n  max-width: 100%;\n  height: auto;\n  display: block;\n  margin: 1rem auto;\n}\n\n/* Background images */\n.hero {\n  background-image: url(\'hero.jpg\');\n  background-size: cover;       /* Cover entire area */\n  background-position: center;  /* Center the image */\n  background-repeat: no-repeat;\n}\n\n/* Different images for different screens */\n.hero {\n  background-image: url(\'hero-mobile.jpg\');\n}\n\n@media (min-width: 768px) {\n  .hero {\n    background-image: url(\'hero-tablet.jpg\');\n  }\n}\n\n@media (min-width: 1200px) {\n  .hero {\n    background-image: url(\'hero-desktop.jpg\');\n  }\n}\n\n/* Art direction with picture element */\n&lt;picture&gt;\n  &lt;source media="(min-width: 800px)" srcset="large.jpg"&gt;\n  &lt;source media="(min-width: 400px)" srcset="medium.jpg"&gt;\n  &lt;img src="small.jpg" alt="Description"&gt;\n&lt;/picture&gt;\n\n/* Responsive images with srcset */\n&lt;img src="small.jpg"\n     srcset="small.jpg 400w,\n             medium.jpg 800w,\n             large.jpg 1200w"\n     sizes="(max-width: 600px) 100vw,\n            (max-width: 1200px) 50vw,\n            400px"\n     alt="Description"&gt;\n\n/* Object-fit for fixed-size containers */\n.thumbnail {\n  width: 200px;\n  height: 200px;\n  object-fit: cover;      /* Crop to fill */\n}\n\n.banner {\n  width: 100%;\n  height: 300px;\n  object-fit: contain;    /* Fit without cropping */\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>6. Responsive Navigation</h2>\n                <p>Navigation patterns that work on all screen sizes.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Desktop: horizontal nav, Mobile: hamburger menu */\n\n/* HTML */\n&lt;nav class="nav"&gt;\n  &lt;button class="nav-toggle" aria-label="Toggle menu"&gt;\n    ☰\n  &lt;/button&gt;\n  &lt;ul class="nav-menu"&gt;\n    &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href="#"&gt;Home&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;\n    &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href="#"&gt;About&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;\n    &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href="#"&gt;Services&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;\n    &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href="#"&gt;Contact&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;\n  &lt;/ul&gt;\n&lt;/nav&gt;\n\n/* CSS - Mobile First */\n.nav {\n  display: flex;\n  justify-content: space-between;\n  align-items: center;\n  padding: 1rem;\n}\n\n.nav-toggle {\n  display: block;      /* Show hamburger on mobile */\n}\n\n.nav-menu {\n  display: none;       /* Hide menu by default on mobile */\n  position: absolute;\n  top: 100%;\n  left: 0;\n  right: 0;\n  background: white;\n  flex-direction: column;\n  padding: 1rem;\n}\n\n.nav-menu.active {\n  display: flex;       /* Show when toggled */\n}\n\n.nav-menu li {\n  margin: 0.5rem 0;\n}\n\n/* Desktop styles */\n@media (min-width: 768px) {\n  .nav-toggle {\n    display: none;     /* Hide hamburger on desktop */\n  }\n  \n  .nav-menu {\n    display: flex;     /* Always show on desktop */\n    position: static;\n    flex-direction: row;\n    gap: 2rem;\n  }\n  \n  .nav-menu li {\n    margin: 0;\n  }\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>7. Responsive Grid and Flexbox</h2>\n                <p>Modern CSS makes responsive layouts easier than ever.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Responsive grid without media queries */\n.card-grid {\n  display: grid;\n  grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(280px, 1fr));\n  gap: 20px;\n}\n/* Automatically adjusts columns based on available space */\n\n/* Responsive flexbox */\n.flex-container {\n  display: flex;\n  flex-wrap: wrap;\n  gap: 20px;\n}\n\n.flex-item {\n  flex: 1 1 300px;    /* Grow, shrink, minimum 300px */\n  max-width: 100%;\n}\n\n/* With media queries for more control */\n.layout {\n  display: grid;\n  grid-template-columns: 1fr;\n  gap: 20px;\n}\n\n@media (min-width: 768px) {\n  .layout {\n    grid-template-columns: 250px 1fr;\n  }\n}\n\n@media (min-width: 1024px) {\n  .layout {\n    grid-template-columns: 250px 1fr 200px;\n  }\n}\n\n/* Responsive font sizes */\n.text {\n  font-size: 1rem;\n}\n\n@media (min-width: 768px) {\n  .text {\n    font-size: 1.125rem;\n  }\n}\n\n/* Or use clamp for automatic scaling */\n.text {\n  font-size: clamp(1rem, 2vw + 0.5rem, 1.25rem);\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>8. Responsive Tables</h2>\n                <p>Tables need special handling on small screens.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Option 1: Horizontal scroll */\n.table-container {\n  overflow-x: auto;\n  -webkit-overflow-scrolling: touch;\n}\n\n/* Option 2: Stack table cells */\n@media (max-width: 600px) {\n  table, thead, tbody, th, td, tr {\n    display: block;\n  }\n  \n  thead {\n    display: none;    /* Hide headers on mobile */\n  }\n  \n  tr {\n    margin-bottom: 1rem;\n    border: 1px solid #ddd;\n  }\n  \n  td {\n    display: flex;\n    justify-content: space-between;\n    padding: 0.5rem;\n    border-bottom: 1px solid #eee;\n  }\n  \n  td::before {\n    content: attr(data-label);\n    font-weight: bold;\n  }\n}\n\n/* HTML */\n&lt;table&gt;\n  &lt;tr&gt;\n    &lt;td data-label="Name"&gt;John Doe&lt;/td&gt;\n    &lt;td data-label="Email"&gt;john@example.com&lt;/td&gt;\n  &lt;/tr&gt;\n&lt;/table&gt;\n\n/* Option 3: Card view on mobile */\n@media (max-width: 600px) {\n  .data-table {\n    display: grid;\n    gap: 1rem;\n  }\n  \n  .data-table tr {\n    display: block;\n    background: #f9f9f9;\n    padding: 1rem;\n    border-radius: 8px;\n  }\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>9. Testing Responsive Design</h2>\n                <p>How to test your responsive designs effectively.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Browser DevTools */\n/* 1. Open DevTools (F12) */\n/* 2. Click device toolbar icon (or Ctrl+Shift+M) */\n/* 3. Select device or enter custom dimensions */\n/* 4. Test different breakpoints */\n\n/* Common device sizes to test: */\n/* - iPhone SE: 375 x 667 */\n/* - iPhone 12: 390 x 844 */\n/* - iPad Mini: 768 x 1024 */\n/* - iPad Pro: 1024 x 1366 */\n/* - Desktop: 1920 x 1080 */\n\n/* Responsive testing tips: */\n/* 1. Test at actual breakpoints */\n/* 2. Test BETWEEN breakpoints */\n/* 3. Test extreme sizes */\n/* 4. Test real devices when possible */\n/* 5. Check touch targets (minimum 44px) */\n\n/* Resize browser window */\n/* Drag browser edge to test fluid layouts */\n\n/* Online tools: */\n/* - Responsively App */\n/* - BrowserStack */\n/* - LambdaTest */</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>10. Responsive Design Checklist</h2>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* ✓ Viewport meta tag included */\n/* ✓ Mobile-first CSS approach */\n/* ✓ Fluid layouts with percentages */\n/* ✓ Flexible images (max-width: 100%) */\n/* ✓ Readable text at all sizes */\n/* ✓ Touch targets large enough (44px minimum) */\n/* ✓ Navigation works on mobile */\n/* ✓ Tables handled on small screens */\n/* ✓ No horizontal scroll at any size */\n/* ✓ Content not cut off */\n/* ✓ Forms usable on mobile */\n/* ✓ Adequate contrast on all backgrounds */</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section class="practice">\n                <h2>🎯 Practice Exercise</h2>\n                <p>Make this layout responsive:</p>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Start with this desktop-only layout: */\n.layout {\n  display: grid;\n  grid-template-columns: 200px 1fr;\n  gap: 20px;\n}\n\n.card-grid {\n  display: grid;\n  grid-template-columns: repeat(4, 1fr);\n  gap: 20px;\n}\n\n/* Make it work on mobile: */\n/* - Single column on mobile */\n/* - Cards stack 2 per row on tablet */\n/* - 4 columns only on desktop */\n\n/* Your CSS: */</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section class="summary">\n                <h2>📚 Key Takeaways</h2>\n                <ul>\n                    <li>Always include the viewport meta tag</li>\n                    <li>Use mobile-first approach with min-width media queries</li>\n                    <li>Make layouts fluid with percentages and fr units</li>\n                    <li>Use clamp() for fluid typography and spacing</li>\n                    <li>max-width: 100% makes images responsive</li>\n                    <li>Test on real devices and various screen sizes</li>\n                    <li>Modern CSS (Grid, Flexbox) reduces media query needs</li>\n                    <li>Consider touch targets and usability on mobile</li>\n                </ul>\n            </section>\n        </div>\n        \n        <div class="lesson-navigation">\n            <a href="lesson8.html" class="btn-secondary">← Previous: CSS Grid</a>\n            <a href="lesson10.html" class="btn-primary">Next: Transitions & Animations →</a>\n        </div>\n    </main>\n    \n    <footer>\n        <p>&copy; 2024 Learner. Transitions create smooth changes between states, while animations enable complex, multi-step motion sequences. Used thoughtfully, they improve user experience by providing visual feedback and guiding attention. Overused, they can distract and annoy.</p>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>1. CSS Transitions</h2>\n                <p>Transitions smoothly animate changes between CSS states.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Basic transition */\n.button {\n  background-color: #7C3AED;\n  transition: background-color 0.3s ease;\n}\n\n.button:hover {\n  background-color: #9333EA;\n}\n/* Background smoothly changes over 0.3 seconds */\n\n/* Transition syntax */\n.element {\n  /* transition: property duration timing-function delay; */\n  transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;\n}\n\n/* Individual properties */\n.element {\n  transition-property: background-color, transform;\n  transition-duration: 0.3s;\n  transition-timing-function: ease;\n  transition-delay: 0s;\n}\n\n/* Multiple transitions */\n.card {\n  transition: \n    background-color 0.3s ease,\n    transform 0.2s ease-out,\n    box-shadow 0.3s ease;\n}\n\n/* Shorthand for multiple */\n.card {\n  transition: all 0.3s ease;    /* All animatable properties */\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="explanation">\n                    <strong>Transition components:</strong>\n                    <ul>\n                        <li><strong>property:</strong> What CSS property to animate (or "all")</li>\n                        <li><strong>duration:</strong> How long the transition takes (0.3s, 300ms)</li>\n                        <li><strong>timing-function:</strong> Speed curve (ease, linear, ease-in, ease-out)</li>\n                        <li><strong>delay:</strong> Wait before starting</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>2. Timing Functions</h2>\n                <p>Timing functions control the acceleration curve of transitions.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Built-in timing functions */\n.ease {\n  transition-timing-function: ease;        /* Default: slow start, fast middle, slow end */\n}\n\n.linear {\n  transition-timing-function: linear;      /* Constant speed */\n}\n\n.ease-in {\n  transition-timing-function: ease-in;     /* Slow start */\n}\n\n.ease-out {\n  transition-timing-function: ease-out;    /* Slow end */\n}\n\n.ease-in-out {\n  transition-timing-function: ease-in-out; /* Slow start and end */\n}\n\n/* Cubic-bezier for custom curves */\n.custom {\n  transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.68, -0.55, 0.27, 1.55);\n  /* Bouncy effect! */\n}\n\n/* Step functions */\n.steps {\n  transition-timing-function: steps(4, end);\n  /* Animation jumps in 4 discrete steps */\n}\n\n/* Common timing function presets */\n:root {\n  --ease-smooth: cubic-bezier(0.25, 0.1, 0.25, 1);\n  --ease-bounce: cubic-bezier(0.68, -0.55, 0.265, 1.55);\n  --ease-elastic: cubic-bezier(0.68, -0.6, 0.32, 1.6);\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <strong>Choosing timing functions:</strong> Use ease-out for elements entering the screen, ease-in for elements leaving, and ease-in-out for state changes.\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>3. Transform Property</h2>\n                <p>Transforms are perfect for transitions — they\'re performant and versatile.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Scale: Grow or shrink */\n.scale-box {\n  transition: transform 0.3s ease;\n}\n\n.scale-box:hover {\n  transform: scale(1.1);        /* Grow 10% */\n  transform: scale(0.9);        /* Shrink 10% */\n  transform: scaleX(1.5);       /* Stretch horizontally */\n  transform: scaleY(0.8);       /* Compress vertically */\n}\n\n/* Rotate: Spin */\n.rotate-box {\n  transition: transform 0.3s ease;\n}\n\n.rotate-box:hover {\n  transform: rotate(45deg);     /* Rotate 45 degrees */\n  transform: rotate(-90deg);    /* Rotate counter-clockwise */\n  transform: rotateX(180deg);   /* 3D rotate around X axis */\n  transform: rotateY(180deg);   /* 3D rotate around Y axis */\n}\n\n/* Translate: Move */\n.move-box {\n  transition: transform 0.3s ease;\n}\n\n.move-box:hover {\n  transform: translateX(20px);  /* Move right 20px */\n  transform: translateY(-10px); /* Move up 10px */\n  transform: translate(20px, -10px);  /* Both X and Y */\n}\n\n/* Skew: Distort */\n.skew-box:hover {\n  transform: skewX(10deg);\n  transform: skewY(5deg);\n  transform: skew(10deg, 5deg);\n}\n\n/* Combine transforms */\n.card {\n  transition: transform 0.3s ease;\n}\n\n.card:hover {\n  transform: translateY(-5px) scale(1.02) rotate(1deg);\n}\n\n/* Transform origin */\n.pivot {\n  transform-origin: center center;    /* Default */\n  transform-origin: top left;\n  transform-origin: 50% 100%;\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="explanation">\n                    <strong>Why transforms for animation:</strong>\n                    <ul>\n                        <li>GPU-accelerated (smooth performance)</li>\n                        <li>Don\'t trigger layout reflows</li>\n                        <li>Can be combined for complex effects</li>\n                        <li>Work great with transitions</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>4. CSS Animations</h2>\n                <p>Keyframe animations create complex, multi-step sequences.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Define keyframes */\n@keyframes fadeIn {\n  from {\n    opacity: 0;\n  }\n  to {\n    opacity: 1;\n  }\n}\n\n/* Or using percentages for more control */\n@keyframes bounce {\n  0% {\n    transform: translateY(0);\n  }\n  50% {\n    transform: translateY(-20px);\n  }\n  100% {\n    transform: translateY(0);\n  }\n}\n\n/* Apply animation */\n.element {\n  animation-name: fadeIn;\n  animation-duration: 1s;\n  animation-timing-function: ease;\n  animation-delay: 0s;\n  animation-iteration-count: 1;\n  animation-direction: normal;\n  animation-fill-mode: forwards;\n  animation-play-state: running;\n}\n\n/* Shorthand */\n.element {\n  /* animation: name duration timing delay count direction fill-mode; */\n  animation: fadeIn 1s ease 0s 1 normal forwards;\n}\n\n/* Multiple animations */\n.element {\n  animation: \n    fadeIn 0.5s ease forwards,\n    slideUp 0.5s ease 0.2s forwards;\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="explanation">\n                    <strong>Animation properties:</strong>\n                    <ul>\n                        <li><strong>name:</strong> The @keyframes name</li>\n                        <li><strong>duration:</strong> How long one cycle takes</li>\n                        <li><strong>timing-function:</strong> Speed curve</li>\n                        <li><strong>delay:</strong> Wait before starting</li>\n                        <li><strong>iteration-count:</strong> How many times (number or infinite)</li>\n                        <li><strong>direction:</strong> normal, reverse, alternate, alternate-reverse</li>\n                        <li><strong>fill-mode:</strong> What happens before/after animation</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>5. Animation Fill Mode</h2>\n                <p>Control what happens before and after an animation.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* none: Default, animation doesn\'t apply outside execution */\n.fill-none {\n  animation-fill-mode: none;\n}\n\n/* forwards: Element keeps final animation state */\n.fill-forwards {\n  animation-fill-mode: forwards;\n}\n/* After animation ends, stays at 100% keyframe state */\n\n/* backwards: Element takes 0% state before delay */\n.fill-backwards {\n  animation-fill-mode: backwards;\n}\n/* During animation delay, takes 0% keyframe state */\n\n/* both: Combines forwards and backwards */\n.fill-both {\n  animation-fill-mode: both;\n}\n\n/* Practical example: Fade in and stay */\n.fade-in {\n  opacity: 0;                          /* Start hidden */\n  animation: fadeIn 1s ease forwards;\n}\n\n@keyframes fadeIn {\n  to {\n    opacity: 1;\n  }\n}\n/* Element fades in and stays visible */</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>6. Common Animation Patterns</h2>\n                \n                <h3>Pulse Effect</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Pulsing element */\n@keyframes pulse {\n  0% {\n    transform: scale(1);\n  }\n  50% {\n    transform: scale(1.1);\n  }\n  100% {\n    transform: scale(1);\n  }\n}\n\n.notification-badge {\n  animation: pulse 2s ease-in-out infinite;\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>Slide In</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Slide in from left */\n@keyframes slideInLeft {\n  from {\n    transform: translateX(-100%);\n    opacity: 0;\n  }\n  to {\n    transform: translateX(0);\n    opacity: 1;\n  }\n}\n\n.slide-in {\n  animation: slideInLeft 0.5s ease-out forwards;\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>Shake Effect</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Shake for errors */\n@keyframes shake {\n  0%, 100% {\n    transform: translateX(0);\n  }\n  10%, 30%, 50%, 70%, 90% {\n    transform: translateX(-5px);\n  }\n  20%, 40%, 60%, 80% {\n    transform: translateX(5px);\n  }\n}\n\n.error-shake {\n  animation: shake 0.5s ease-in-out;\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>Loading Spinner</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Rotating spinner */\n@keyframes spin {\n  from {\n    transform: rotate(0deg);\n  }\n  to {\n    transform: rotate(360deg);\n  }\n}\n\n.spinner {\n  width: 40px;\n  height: 40px;\n  border: 3px solid #e0e0e0;\n  border-top-color: #7C3AED;\n  border-radius: 50%;\n  animation: spin 1s linear infinite;\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <h3>Bounce In</h3>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Bouncy entrance */\n@keyframes bounceIn {\n  0% {\n    opacity: 0;\n    transform: scale(0.3);\n  }\n  50% {\n    transform: scale(1.05);\n  }\n  70% {\n    transform: scale(0.9);\n  }\n  100% {\n    opacity: 1;\n    transform: scale(1);\n  }\n}\n\n.bounce-in {\n  animation: bounceIn 0.6s ease-out forwards;\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>7. Hover Effects</h2>\n                <p>Interactive hover animations enhance user feedback.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Button lift effect */\n.btn {\n  transition: transform 0.3s ease, box-shadow 0.3s ease;\n}\n\n.btn:hover {\n  transform: translateY(-3px);\n  box-shadow: 0 10px 20px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);\n}\n\n/* Image zoom */\n.image-container {\n  overflow: hidden;\n}\n\n.image-container img {\n  transition: transform 0.5s ease;\n}\n\n.image-container:hover img {\n  transform: scale(1.1);\n}\n\n/* Card flip */\n.card {\n  perspective: 1000px;\n}\n\n.card-inner {\n  transition: transform 0.6s;\n  transform-style: preserve-3d;\n}\n\n.card:hover .card-inner {\n  transform: rotateY(180deg);\n}\n\n.card-front, .card-back {\n  backface-visibility: hidden;\n}\n\n.card-back {\n  transform: rotateY(180deg);\n}\n\n/* Underline animation */\n.nav-link {\n  position: relative;\n}\n\n.nav-link::after {\n  content: \'\';\n  position: absolute;\n  bottom: 0;\n  left: 0;\n  width: 0;\n  height: 2px;\n  background: #7C3AED;\n  transition: width 0.3s ease;\n}\n\n.nav-link:hover::after {\n  width: 100%;\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>8. Performance Considerations</h2>\n                <p>Animate efficiently for smooth performance.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Good properties to animate (GPU accelerated) */\n.performant {\n  /* These trigger compositing, not layout: */\n  transform: translateX(10px);    /* ✓ Good */\n  opacity: 0.5;                   /* ✓ Good */\n}\n\n/* Avoid animating these (trigger layout): */\n.avoid {\n  width: 200px;                   /* ✗ Triggers layout */\n  height: 100px;                  /* ✗ Triggers layout */\n  left: 50px;                     /* ✗ Triggers layout */\n  margin: 20px;                   /* ✗ Triggers layout */\n  padding: 10px;                  /* ✗ Triggers layout */\n  border-width: 2px;              /* ✗ Triggers layout */\n}\n\n/* Use will-change sparingly */\n.will-change-element {\n  will-change: transform, opacity;\n}\n/* Tells browser to optimize for these changes */\n/* Only use when you know animation will happen */\n\n/* Reduce motion for accessibility */\n@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) {\n  *,\n  *::before,\n  *::after {\n    animation-duration: 0.01ms !important;\n    animation-iteration-count: 1 !important;\n    transition-duration: 0.01ms !important;\n  }\n}\n\n/* This respects user\'s motion preferences */</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <strong>Performance tip:</strong> Stick to transform and opacity for animations. They\'re GPU-accelerated and won\'t cause layout thrashing.\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>9. Animation Events (JavaScript)</h2>\n                <p>Detect when animations start, end, or repeat.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* JavaScript can listen for animation events */\n/*\n  animationstart - Animation begins\n  animationend - Animation completes\n  animationiteration - Animation repeats\n*/\n\n// JavaScript example\nconst element = document.querySelector(\'.animated\');\n\nelement.addEventListener(\'animationend\', () => {\n  console.log(\'Animation complete!\');\n  element.classList.add(\'animation-done\');\n});\n\n// Start animation by adding class\nfunction startAnimation() {\n  element.classList.add(\'animate\');\n}\n\n// Pause/resume animation\nfunction pauseAnimation() {\n  element.style.animationPlayState = \'paused\';\n}\n\nfunction resumeAnimation() {\n  element.style.animationPlayState = \'running\';\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section class="practice">\n                <h2>🎯 Practice Exercise</h2>\n                <p>Create these animations:</p>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Challenge: Create these effects */\n\n/* 1. A button that grows slightly on hover */\n/* 2. A card that lifts up with shadow on hover */\n/* 3. A loading spinner using animation */\n/* 4. An element that fades in when page loads */\n\n/* Your CSS: */</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section class="summary">\n                <h2>📚 Key Takeaways</h2>\n                <ul>\n                    <li>Transitions smoothly animate between states</li>\n                    <li>transition: property duration timing delay</li>\n                    <li>Transform (scale, rotate, translate) is performant for animation</li>\n                    <li>@keyframes define multi-step animations</li>\n                    <li>animation: name duration timing delay count direction fill</li>\n                    <li>Use fill-mode: forwards to keep final animation state</li>\n                    <li>Stick to transform and opacity for best performance</li>\n                    <li>Respect prefers-reduced-motion for accessibility</li>\n                </ul>\n            </section>\n        </div>\n        \n        <div class="lesson-navigation">\n            <a href="lesson9.html" class="btn-secondary">← Previous: Responsive Design</a>\n            <a href="lesson11.html" class="btn-primary">Next: CSS Variables & Functions →</a>\n        </div>\n    </main>\n    \n    <footer>\n        <p>&copy; 2024 Learner. Combined with CSS functions like calc(), clamp(), and min/max, they enable dynamic, maintainable styling that was previously only possible with CSS preprocessors or JavaScript.</p>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>1. CSS Custom Properties (Variables)</h2>\n                <p>Define reusable values that can be changed in one place.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Define custom properties with -- prefix */\n:root {\n  --primary-color: #7C3AED;\n  --secondary-color: #9333EA;\n  --spacing: 1rem;\n  --border-radius: 8px;\n  --font-family: \'Segoe UI\', Arial, sans-serif;\n}\n\n/* Use with var() function */\n.button {\n  background-color: var(--primary-color);\n  padding: var(--spacing);\n  border-radius: var(--border-radius);\n  font-family: var(--font-family);\n}\n\n/* Fallback values */\n.element {\n  color: var(--text-color, #333);    /* Use #333 if --text-color not defined */\n}\n\n/* Nested fallbacks */\n.element {\n  color: var(--text-color, var(--default-color, black));\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="explanation">\n                    <strong>Why use custom properties:</strong>\n                    <ul>\n                        <li>Change values in one place, update everywhere</li>\n                        <li>Create theming systems easily</li>\n                        <li>Can be manipulated with JavaScript</li>\n                        <li>Cascade and inherit like other properties</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>2. Scope and Inheritance</h2>\n                <p>Custom properties follow CSS cascade and inheritance rules.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Global scope: defined on :root */\n:root {\n  --primary: #7C3AED;\n  --spacing: 1rem;\n}\n\n/* Local scope: defined on specific selector */\n.card {\n  --card-padding: 1.5rem;\n  padding: var(--card-padding);\n}\n\n/* Inheritance: children inherit custom properties */\n.parent {\n  --text-color: #333;\n}\n\n.child {\n  color: var(--text-color);    /* Inherits from parent */\n}\n\n/* Override values locally */\n:root {\n  --background: white;\n}\n\n.dark-mode {\n  --background: #1a1a1a;       /* Override for dark mode */\n}\n\nbody {\n  background-color: var(--background);\n}\n\n/* Scoped components */\n.alert {\n  --alert-color: #7C3AED;\n  border-left: 4px solid var(--alert-color);\n}\n\n.alert.error {\n  --alert-color: #ef4444;\n}\n\n.alert.success {\n  --alert-color: #22c55e;\n}\n/* Each alert type uses its own color */</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <strong>Best practice:</strong> Define design tokens (colors, spacing, typography) on :root for global access. Define component-specific variables within the component selector.\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>3. calc() Function</h2>\n                <p>Perform calculations directly in CSS.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Basic math operations */\n.element {\n  width: calc(100% - 20px);           /* Subtract */\n  width: calc(50% + 10px);            /* Add */\n  width: calc(200px * 2);             /* Multiply */\n  width: calc(600px / 3);             /* Divide */\n}\n\n/* Mix units */\n.container {\n  width: calc(100% - 2rem);           /* Percentage minus rem */\n  padding: calc(1rem + 5px);          /* Mix rem and px */\n}\n\n/* With variables */\n:root {\n  --sidebar-width: 250px;\n}\n\n.main-content {\n  width: calc(100% - var(--sidebar-width));\n}\n\n/* Header height minus padding */\n.header {\n  height: calc(100vh - var(--header-height));\n}\n\n/* Nested calculations */\n.element {\n  width: calc(calc(100% / 3) - 20px);\n  /* Or simply: */\n  width: calc(100% / 3 - 20px);\n}\n\n/* Practical examples */\n\n/* Full-height layout minus fixed header */\nmain {\n  min-height: calc(100vh - 60px);\n}\n\n/* Responsive font size with minimum */\n.text {\n  font-size: calc(1rem + 1vw);\n}\n\n/* Grid gap accounting */\n.item {\n  width: calc(33.333% - 20px);    /* Third minus gap */\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="explanation">\n                    <strong>calc() rules:</strong>\n                    <ul>\n                        <li>Mix different units (%, px, em, rem, vh, vw)</li>\n                        <li>Spaces required around + and - operators</li>\n                        <li>Nested calc() allowed but not necessary</li>\n                        <li>Can use with custom properties</li>\n                    </ul>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>4. min() and max() Functions</h2>\n                <p>Choose the smaller or larger value automatically.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* min(): Use the smallest value */\n.element {\n  width: min(50%, 400px);    /* At most 400px or 50%, whichever is smaller */\n  /* On narrow screens: uses 50% */\n  /* On wide screens: caps at 400px */\n}\n\n/* max(): Use the largest value */\n.element {\n  width: max(300px, 50%);    /* At least 300px or 50%, whichever is larger */\n}\n\n/* Practical example: Responsive container */\n.container {\n  width: min(90%, 1200px);    /* 90% up to max 1200px */\n  margin: 0 auto;\n}\n\n/* Font sizing */\n.text {\n  font-size: max(1rem, 2vw);    /* At least 1rem, scales with viewport */\n}\n\n/* Padding that scales */\n.section {\n  padding: min(5vw, 3rem);      /* Responsive padding with maximum */\n}\n\n/* Multiple values */\n.element {\n  width: min(100%, 800px, 50vw);    /* Uses smallest of all three */\n}\n\n/* With variables */\n:root {\n  --max-width: 1200px;\n  --padding: 2rem;\n}\n\n.container {\n  width: min(var(--max-width), 100% - var(--padding) * 2);\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>5. clamp() Function</h2>\n                <p>Set a value with minimum, preferred, and maximum bounds.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* clamp(min, preferred, max) */\n.element {\n  /* Minimum: 100px\n     Preferred: 50%\n     Maximum: 500px */\n  width: clamp(100px, 50%, 500px);\n}\n\n/* Fluid typography */\nh1 {\n  /* At least 1.5rem, prefers 5vw, at most 3rem */\n  font-size: clamp(1.5rem, 5vw, 3rem);\n}\n\nh2 {\n  font-size: clamp(1.25rem, 4vw, 2.5rem);\n}\n\np {\n  font-size: clamp(1rem, 2vw, 1.25rem);\n}\n\n/* Fluid spacing */\n.section {\n  padding: clamp(1rem, 5vw, 4rem);\n  gap: clamp(1rem, 3vw, 2rem);\n}\n\n/* Fluid width container */\n.container {\n  width: clamp(300px, 90%, 1200px);\n  margin: 0 auto;\n}\n\n/* Fluid line height */\np {\n  line-height: clamp(1.4, 1.5 + 0.5vw, 1.8);\n}\n\n/* Creating a scale system */\n:root {\n  --space-xs: clamp(0.25rem, 1vw, 0.5rem);\n  --space-sm: clamp(0.5rem, 2vw, 1rem);\n  --space-md: clamp(1rem, 3vw, 1.5rem);\n  --space-lg: clamp(1.5rem, 4vw, 2rem);\n  --space-xl: clamp(2rem, 5vw, 3rem);\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <strong>Why clamp is powerful:</strong> It replaces media queries for many responsive sizing needs. One line of CSS creates fluid scaling with built-in limits.\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>6. Color Functions</h2>\n                <p>Modern CSS provides powerful color manipulation functions.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* rgb() and rgba() */\n.element {\n  color: rgb(124, 58, 237);              /* Purple */\n  color: rgba(124, 58, 237, 0.8);        /* With 80% opacity */\n  /* Modern syntax: */\n  color: rgb(124 58 237);                /* No commas */\n  color: rgb(124 58 237 / 0.8);          /* Alpha with slash */\n}\n\n/* hsl() and hsla() */\n.element {\n  color: hsl(258, 83%, 58%);\n  color: hsla(258, 83%, 58%, 0.8);\n  /* Modern syntax: */\n  color: hsl(258 83% 58%);\n  color: hsl(258 83% 58% / 0.8);\n}\n\n/* Mixing colors */\n.mixed {\n  background-color: color-mix(in srgb, #7C3AED 50%, white);\n  /* Mixes purple with white at 50% */\n}\n\n/* Relative color syntax (new!) */\n:root {\n  --primary: #7C3AED;\n  \n  /* Create variations from base color */\n  --primary-light: hsl(from var(--primary) h s 80%);\n  --primary-dark: hsl(from var(--primary) h s 30%);\n  --primary-transparent: hsl(from var(--primary) h s l / 0.5);\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>7. Environment Variables</h2>\n                <p>Access browser and device information with env().</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Safe area insets for notched devices */\n.element {\n  /* Add padding for device notch/safe areas */\n  padding: env(safe-area-inset-top);\n  padding-bottom: env(safe-area-inset-bottom);\n  padding-left: env(safe-area-inset-left);\n  padding-right: env(safe-area-inset-right);\n}\n\n/* Full screen app on iPhone */\n.app {\n  padding-top: env(safe-area-inset-top, 20px);\n  /* Fallback of 20px if env() not supported */\n}\n\n/* Combining with calc */\n.footer {\n  padding-bottom: calc(1rem + env(safe-area-inset-bottom));\n}\n\n/* For web app manifests */\nbody {\n  display: grid;\n  grid-template-rows: auto 1fr auto;\n  min-height: 100vh;\n  min-height: 100dvh;    /* Dynamic viewport height */\n  padding-bottom: env(safe-area-inset-bottom);\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="explanation">\n                    <strong>When to use env():</strong> Essential for apps on iOS devices with notches. Ensures content isn\'t hidden behind the notch or home indicator.\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>8. Custom Properties with JavaScript</h2>\n                <p>Dynamically update CSS variables from JavaScript.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* CSS */\n:root {\n  --primary-color: #7C3AED;\n  --rotation: 0deg;\n}\n\n.box {\n  background: var(--primary-color);\n  transform: rotate(var(--rotation));\n}\n\n/* JavaScript */\n// Get computed value\nconst primaryColor = getComputedStyle(document.documentElement)\n  .getPropertyValue(\'--primary-color\');\n\n// Set value on root\ndocument.documentElement.style.setProperty(\'--primary-color\', \'#9333EA\');\n\n// Set value on specific element\nconst card = document.querySelector(\'.card\');\ncard.style.setProperty(\'--rotation\', \'45deg\');\n\n// Toggle dark mode\nfunction toggleDarkMode() {\n  const root = document.documentElement;\n  const currentTheme = getComputedStyle(root).getPropertyValue(\'--bg-color\');\n  \n  if (currentTheme === \'#ffffff\') {\n    root.style.setProperty(\'--bg-color\', \'#1a1a1a\');\n    root.style.setProperty(\'--text-color\', \'#ffffff\');\n  } else {\n    root.style.setProperty(\'--bg-color\', \'#ffffff\');\n    root.style.setProperty(\'--text-color\', \'#1a1a1a\');\n  }\n}\n\n// Slider controls rotation\nslider.addEventListener(\'input\', (e) => {\n  document.documentElement.style.setProperty(\'--rotation\', `${e.target.value}deg`);\n});</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>9. Building a Design System</h2>\n                <p>Use custom properties to create maintainable design tokens.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Design Tokens */\n:root {\n  /* Colors */\n  --color-primary: #7C3AED;\n  --color-primary-light: #A78BFA;\n  --color-primary-dark: #6D28D9;\n  --color-secondary: #9333EA;\n  --color-success: #22C55E;\n  --color-warning: #EAB308;\n  --color-error: #EF4444;\n  \n  /* Neutrals */\n  --color-white: #FFFFFF;\n  --color-gray-100: #F3F4F6;\n  --color-gray-200: #E5E7EB;\n  --color-gray-300: #D1D5DB;\n  --color-gray-500: #6B7280;\n  --color-gray-700: #374151;\n  --color-gray-900: #111827;\n  \n  /* Typography */\n  --font-family-base: \'Inter\', system-ui, sans-serif;\n  --font-family-mono: \'Fira Code\', monospace;\n  --font-size-xs: 0.75rem;\n  --font-size-sm: 0.875rem;\n  --font-size-base: 1rem;\n  --font-size-lg: 1.125rem;\n  --font-size-xl: 1.25rem;\n  --font-size-2xl: 1.5rem;\n  --font-size-3xl: 2rem;\n  \n  /* Spacing */\n  --space-1: 0.25rem;\n  --space-2: 0.5rem;\n  --space-3: 0.75rem;\n  --space-4: 1rem;\n  --space-6: 1.5rem;\n  --space-8: 2rem;\n  --space-12: 3rem;\n  --space-16: 4rem;\n  \n  /* Shadows */\n  --shadow-sm: 0 1px 2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05);\n  --shadow-md: 0 4px 6px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1);\n  --shadow-lg: 0 10px 15px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1);\n  \n  /* Border radius */\n  --radius-sm: 0.25rem;\n  --radius-md: 0.5rem;\n  --radius-lg: 1rem;\n  --radius-full: 9999px;\n  \n  /* Transitions */\n  --transition-fast: 150ms ease;\n  --transition-base: 300ms ease;\n  --transition-slow: 500ms ease;\n}\n\n/* Using the design system */\n.button {\n  background: var(--color-primary);\n  padding: var(--space-2) var(--space-4);\n  border-radius: var(--radius-md);\n  font-size: var(--font-size-base);\n  transition: background-color var(--transition-fast);\n}\n\n.button:hover {\n  background: var(--color-primary-dark);\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section class="practice">\n                <h2>🎯 Practice Exercise</h2>\n                <p>Create a design system using CSS variables:</p>\n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Challenge: Build a complete design system */\n\n/* 1. Define color variables (primary, secondary, neutrals) */\n/* 2. Create spacing scale using variables */\n/* 3. Build a button component using only variables */\n/* 4. Use clamp() for responsive font sizes */\n\n/* Your CSS: */</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section class="summary">\n                <h2>📚 Key Takeaways</h2>\n                <ul>\n                    <li>Custom properties (--name) store reusable values</li>\n                    <li>var() retrieves values with optional fallbacks</li>\n                    <li>Custom properties cascade and inherit</li>\n                    <li>calc() performs calculations mixing units</li>\n                    <li>min() and max() choose between values</li>\n                    <li>clamp(min, preferred, max) sets bounded values</li>\n                    <li>Use clamp() for fluid typography and spacing</li>\n                    <li>Custom properties can be modified with JavaScript</li>\n                    <li>Build design systems with CSS variables as tokens</li>\n                </ul>\n            </section>\n        </div>\n        \n        <div class="lesson-navigation">\n            <a href="lesson10.html" class="btn-secondary">← Previous: Transitions & Animations</a>\n            <a href="lesson12.html" class="btn-primary">Next: Best Practices & Architecture →</a>\n        </div>\n    </main>\n    \n    <footer>\n        <p>&copy; 2024 Learner. This lesson covers industry best practices, naming conventions, and architectural patterns that help you write scalable, maintainable CSS. These techniques are used by professional developers and large teams to keep CSS manageable even in massive projects.</p>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>1. CSS Organization Strategies</h2>\n                <p>Organizing your CSS files makes code easier to find and maintain.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Common file organization approaches */\n\n/* Option 1: By page/section */\n/*\n  styles/\n  ├── main.css          (imports all others)\n  ├── header.css\n  ├── footer.css\n  ├── home.css\n  ├── about.css\n  └── contact.css\n*/\n\n/* Option 2: By component (recommended) */\n/*\n  styles/\n  ├── main.css          (imports all others)\n  ├── base/\n  │   ├── reset.css\n  │   ├── typography.css\n  │   └── variables.css\n  ├── components/\n  │   ├── button.css\n  │   ├── card.css\n  │   ├── navigation.css\n  │   └── form.css\n  ├── layout/\n  │   ├── grid.css\n  │   ├── header.css\n  │   └── footer.css\n  └── utilities/\n      └── utilities.css\n*/\n\n/* Option 3: 7-1 Pattern (popular) */\n/*\n  styles/\n  ├── main.css\n  ├── abstracts/\n  │   ├── _variables.css\n  │   ├── _mixins.css\n  │   └── _functions.css\n  ├── base/\n  │   ├── _reset.css\n  │   └── _typography.css\n  ├── components/\n  │   ├── _button.css\n  │   └── _card.css\n  ├── layout/\n  │   ├── _header.css\n  │   └── _footer.css\n  ├── pages/\n  │   └── _home.css\n  ├── themes/\n  │   └── _default.css\n  └── vendors/\n      └── _normalize.css\n*/</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>2. Naming Conventions</h2>\n                <p>Consistent naming makes CSS predictable and self-documenting.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* BEM (Block Element Modifier) - Most popular */\n/* Block: Standalone component */\n/* Element: Part of a block */\n/* Modifier: Variation of a block/element */\n\n.card { }                    /* Block */\n.card__header { }            /* Element */\n.card__body { }              /* Element */\n.card__footer { }            /* Element */\n.card--featured { }          /* Modifier */\n.card--dark { }              /* Modifier */\n.card__header--highlighted { }  /* Element modifier */\n\n/* HTML */\n&lt;div class="card card--featured"&gt;\n  &lt;div class="card__header"&gt;...&lt;/div&gt;\n  &lt;div class="card__body"&gt;...&lt;/div&gt;\n&lt;/div&gt;\n\n/* Why BEM works: */\n/* - Clear relationship between HTML and CSS */\n/* - Flat selector specificity (no deep nesting) */\n/* - Reusable, modular components */\n/* - Easy to understand structure */\n\n/* Other conventions */\n\n/* SMACSS (Scalable and Modular Architecture) */\n/* Categories: Base, Layout, Module, State, Theme */\n.layout-header { }\n.is-active { }\n.is-hidden { }\n\n/* OOCSS (Object-Oriented CSS) */\n/* Separate structure from skin */\n.btn {              /* Structure */\n  display: inline-block;\n  padding: 10px 20px;\n}\n.btn-primary {      /* Skin */\n  background: #7C3AED;\n  color: white;\n}\n\n/* Utility-first (like Tailwind) */\n.mt-4 { margin-top: 1rem; }\n.p-2 { padding: 0.5rem; }\n.text-center { text-align: center; }</code></pre>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <strong>Why naming conventions matter:</strong> They prevent naming conflicts, make code searchable, and help team members understand each other\'s code.\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>3. Specificity Management</h2>\n                <p>Keep specificity low and predictable for easier overrides.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Specificity hierarchy (lowest to highest) */\n/* 1. Element selectors:       0-0-1 */\n/* 2. Class selectors:          0-1-0 */\n/* 3. ID selectors:             1-0-0 */\n/* 4. Inline styles:            1-0-0-0 */\n/* 5. !important:               Highest */\n\n/* Bad: High specificity selectors */\n#header .nav ul li a { }          /* 1-0-3 - too high! */\ndiv.wrapper div.content p { }     /* 0-0-5 - inefficient! */\n\n/* Good: Low specificity selectors */\n.nav-link { }                     /* 0-1-0 - simple! */\n.content-text { }                 /* 0-1-0 - predictable! */\n\n/* The "Inverted Triangle" CSS approach */\n/* 1. Generic styles first (low specificity) */\n/* 2. Component styles middle */\n/* 3. Utility/override styles last */\n\n/* Use classes, avoid IDs for styling */\n/* Bad */\n#main-header { }                  /* Hard to override */\n\n/* Good */\n.header { }                       /* Easy to override */\n.header--dark { }                 /* Modifier extends without conflict */\n\n/* Avoid !important unless absolutely necessary */\n/* Only acceptable uses: */\n/* - Utility classes that must always win */\n/* - Overriding third-party CSS you can\'t control */\n\n.hidden {\n  display: none !important;       /* Utility that must always work */\n}\n\n/* Managing deep nesting - DON\'T DO THIS: */\n.sidebar .widget .list .item .link {\n  color: #7C3AED;\n}\n\n/* DO THIS instead: */\n.sidebar-link {\n  color: #7C3AED;\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>4. CSS Reset vs Normalize</h2>\n                <p>Start with consistent browser defaults.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* CSS Reset - Strip all defaults */\n/* Simple reset */\n*, *::before, *::after {\n  box-sizing: border-box;\n  margin: 0;\n  padding: 0;\n}\n\n/* Modern CSS Reset */\n/* 1. Use box-sizing: border-box globally */\n*, *::before, *::after {\n  box-sizing: border-box;\n}\n\n/* 2. Remove default margins */\nbody, h1, h2, h3, h4, p, figure, blockquote, dl, dd {\n  margin: 0;\n}\n\n/* 3. Set core root defaults */\nhtml:focus-within {\n  scroll-behavior: smooth;\n}\n\n/* 4. Set core body defaults */\nbody {\n  min-height: 100vh;\n  text-rendering: optimizeSpeed;\n  line-height: 1.5;\n}\n\n/* 5. Remove list styles */\nul[role=\'list\'], ol[role=\'list\'] {\n  list-style: none;\n}\n\n/* 6. Make images easier to work with */\nimg, picture, video, canvas, svg {\n  display: block;\n  max-width: 100%;\n}\n\n/* 7. Remove built-in form typography styles */\ninput, button, textarea, select {\n  font: inherit;\n}\n\n/* 8. Remove animations for those who prefer */\n@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) {\n  html:focus-within {\n    scroll-behavior: auto;\n  }\n  *, *::before, *::after {\n    animation-duration: 0.01ms !important;\n    animation-iteration-count: 1 !important;\n    transition-duration: 0.01ms !important;\n    scroll-behavior: auto !important;\n  }\n}\n\n/* Normalize.css approach */\n/* Instead of stripping, make defaults consistent */\n/* Include via CDN or npm */</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>5. Component-Based CSS</h2>\n                <p>Write self-contained, reusable component styles.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Component structure */\n.card {\n  /* 1. Component variables */\n  --card-padding: 1.5rem;\n  --card-radius: 8px;\n  --card-shadow: 0 4px 6px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1);\n  \n  /* 2. Base styles */\n  background: white;\n  border-radius: var(--card-radius);\n  box-shadow: var(--card-shadow);\n  overflow: hidden;\n}\n\n/* 3. Elements */\n.card__header {\n  padding: var(--card-padding);\n  border-bottom: 1px solid #eee;\n}\n\n.card__image {\n  width: 100%;\n  aspect-ratio: 16/9;\n  object-fit: cover;\n}\n\n.card__body {\n  padding: var(--card-padding);\n}\n\n.card__title {\n  font-size: 1.25rem;\n  margin-bottom: 0.5rem;\n}\n\n.card__text {\n  color: #666;\n  line-height: 1.6;\n}\n\n.card__footer {\n  padding: var(--card-padding);\n  border-top: 1px solid #eee;\n  display: flex;\n  justify-content: space-between;\n}\n\n/* 4. Modifiers */\n.card--featured {\n  border: 2px solid var(--primary);\n}\n\n.card--dark {\n  background: #1a1a1a;\n  color: white;\n}\n\n.card--dark .card__text {\n  color: #aaa;\n}\n\n/* 5. States */\n.card.is-loading {\n  opacity: 0.6;\n  pointer-events: none;\n}\n\n.card.is-selected {\n  outline: 2px solid var(--primary);\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>6. Utility Classes</h2>\n                <p>Small, single-purpose classes for common adjustments.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Spacing utilities */\n.m-0 { margin: 0; }\n.m-1 { margin: 0.25rem; }\n.m-2 { margin: 0.5rem; }\n.m-4 { margin: 1rem; }\n.m-8 { margin: 2rem; }\n\n.mt-0 { margin-top: 0; }\n.mt-4 { margin-top: 1rem; }\n.mb-4 { margin-bottom: 1rem; }\n\n.p-0 { padding: 0; }\n.p-4 { padding: 1rem; }\n.px-4 { padding-left: 1rem; padding-right: 1rem; }\n.py-4 { padding-top: 1rem; padding-bottom: 1rem; }\n\n/* Flexbox utilities */\n.flex { display: flex; }\n.flex-col { flex-direction: column; }\n.items-center { align-items: center; }\n.justify-center { justify-content: center; }\n.justify-between { justify-content: space-between; }\n.gap-4 { gap: 1rem; }\n\n/* Text utilities */\n.text-center { text-align: center; }\n.text-left { text-align: left; }\n.text-right { text-align: right; }\n.font-bold { font-weight: 700; }\n.text-sm { font-size: 0.875rem; }\n.text-lg { font-size: 1.125rem; }\n\n/* Color utilities */\n.text-primary { color: var(--color-primary); }\n.text-muted { color: var(--color-gray-500); }\n.bg-primary { background-color: var(--color-primary); }\n\n/* Display utilities */\n.hidden { display: none; }\n.block { display: block; }\n.inline-block { display: inline-block; }\n\n/* Responsive utilities */\n@media (min-width: 768px) {\n  .md\\:hidden { display: none; }\n  .md\\:block { display: block; }\n  .md\\:flex { display: flex; }\n}\n\n/* Usage in HTML */\n&lt;div class="flex items-center justify-between p-4 bg-primary"&gt;\n  &lt;h2 class="text-lg font-bold"&gt;Title&lt;/h2&gt;\n  &lt;button class="btn btn-secondary"&gt;Action&lt;/button&gt;\n&lt;/div&gt;</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>7. CSS Architecture Patterns</h2>\n                <p>Proven patterns for organizing large CSS codebases.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* ITCSS (Inverted Triangle CSS) */\n/* Layers from generic to specific: */\n\n/* 1. Settings - Variables, configs */\n:root {\n  --color-primary: #7C3AED;\n}\n\n/* 2. Tools - Mixins, functions (if using preprocessor) */\n\n/* 3. Generic - Reset, normalize */\n* { box-sizing: border-box; }\n\n/* 4. Elements - Base HTML elements */\nbody {\n  font-family: system-ui, sans-serif;\n  line-height: 1.5;\n}\n\nh1, h2, h3 {\n  margin: 0;\n}\n\n/* 5. Objects - Layout patterns */\n.container {\n  max-width: 1200px;\n  margin: 0 auto;\n}\n\n.grid {\n  display: grid;\n  gap: 1rem;\n}\n\n/* 6. Components - UI components */\n.btn {\n  display: inline-block;\n  padding: 0.5rem 1rem;\n}\n\n.card {\n  background: white;\n  border-radius: 8px;\n}\n\n/* 7. Utilities - Helper classes */\n.mt-4 { margin-top: 1rem; }\n.text-center { text-align: center; }\n\n/* CUBE CSS (newer approach) */\n/* C - Composition: Layout structures */\n/* U - Utilities: Single-purpose classes */\n/* B - Blocks: Components */\n/* E - Exceptions: Variations */\n\n/* Layer order in main.css */\n@import \'settings.css\';\n@import \'generic.css\';\n@import \'elements.css\';\n@import \'objects.css\';\n@import \'components.css\';\n@import \'utilities.css\';</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>8. Performance Best Practices</h2>\n                <p>Optimize CSS for faster loading and rendering.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* 1. Minimize CSS size */\n/* - Remove unused styles */\n/* - Minify for production */\n/* - Use short class names in production */\n\n/* 2. Avoid expensive selectors */\n/* Bad: Forces browser to check all elements */\n[class*="button"] { }\n\n/* Good: Simple class selector */\n.btn { }\n\n/* 3. Reduce layout thrashing */\n/* Properties that trigger layout: */\n/* width, height, padding, margin, top, left, font-size */\n\n/* Use transform for animations instead */\n.moving-element {\n  transform: translateX(100px);  /* Doesn\'t trigger layout */\n}\n\n/* 4. Use will-change sparingly */\n.will-animate {\n  will-change: transform;  /* Only for elements that WILL animate */\n}\n\n/* 5. Critical CSS inline */\n/* Inline above-the-fold CSS for faster first paint */\n&lt;head&gt;\n  &lt;style&gt;\n    /* Critical CSS here */\n    body { margin: 0; }\n    .header { position: sticky; }\n  &lt;/style&gt;\n  &lt;link rel="stylesheet" href="styles.css"&gt;\n&lt;/head&gt;\n\n/* 6. Lazy load non-critical CSS */\n&lt;link rel="stylesheet" href="print.css" media="print"&gt;\n&lt;link rel="stylesheet" href="large.css" media="(min-width: 1200px)"&gt;\n\n/* 7. Use content-visibility for off-screen content */\n.long-list-item {\n  content-visibility: auto;  /* Skip rendering until visible */\n  contain-intrinsic-size: 200px;  /* Estimated height */\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>9. CSS Validation and Debugging</h2>\n                <p>Tools and techniques for maintaining CSS quality.</p>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Browser DevTools */\n/* 1. Inspect element styles */\n/* 2. See computed values */\n/* 3. Check cascade order */\n/* 4. Toggle styles on/off */\n/* 5. Edit values live */\n\n/* Common issues to debug: */\n\n/* Element not styling? */\n/* - Check specificity */\n/* - Look for typos */\n/* - Verify selector matches */\n/* - Check for conflicts */\n\n/* Layout broken? */\n/* - Use box-sizing: border-box */\n/* - Check for collapsed margins */\n/* - Look for overflow issues */\n/* - Verify flex/grid properties */\n\n/* Debugging with outlines */\n* {\n  outline: 1px solid red;  /* Visualize all elements */\n}\n\n/* CSS Validation */\n/* - W3C CSS Validator: https://jigsaw.w3.org/css-validator/ */\n/* - Browser DevTools console shows errors */\n\n/* Linting with stylelint */\n/* .stylelintrc configuration */\n{\n  "extends": "stylelint-config-standard",\n  "rules": {\n    "color-hex-length": "short",\n    "selector-class-pattern": "^[a-z][a-z0-9]*(-[a-z0-9]+)*$"\n  }\n}</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section>\n                <h2>10. CSS Checklist</h2>\n                \n                <div class="code-block">\n                    <pre><code>/* Before shipping CSS: */\n\n/* ✓ Organization */\n/*   - Files organized logically */\n/*   - Consistent naming convention */\n/*   - Comments for complex sections */\n\n/* ✓ Performance */\n/*   - No unused styles */\n/*   - Minimal specificity */\n/*   - Critical CSS inlined */\n\n/* ✓ Maintainability */\n/*   - Variables for repeated values */\n/*   - Components are reusable */\n/*   - Easy to find and update */\n\n/* ✓ Accessibility */\n/*   - Sufficient color contrast */\n/*   - Focus styles present */\n/*   - prefers-reduced-motion respected */\n\n/* ✓ Browser Support */\n/*   - Vendor prefixes where needed */\n/*   - Fallbacks for newer features */\n/*   - Tested in target browsers */\n\n/* ✓ Responsive */\n/*   - Mobile-first approach */\n/*   - Tested at various breakpoints */\n/*   - Flexible layouts */\n\n/* ✓ Code Quality */\n/*   - Consistent formatting */\n/*   - No !important abuse */\n/*   - Valid CSS syntax */</code></pre>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section class="conclusion">\n                <h2>🎉 Congratulations!</h2>\n                <p>You\'ve completed the CSS Course! You\'ve learned everything from basic selectors and colors to advanced topics like Grid, animations, and professional architecture patterns. You now have the knowledge to style beautiful, responsive, and maintainable websites.</p>\n                \n                <div class="tip-box">\n                    <strong>What\'s next?</strong>\n                    <p>Continue your learning journey with the <strong>JavaScript Course</strong> to add interactivity and dynamic behavior to your websites.</p>\n                </div>\n            </section>\n            \n            <section class="summary">\n                <h2>📚 Key Takeaways</h2>\n                <ul>\n                    <li>Organize CSS files by component or layer</li>\n                    <li>Use naming conventions like BEM for clarity</li>\n                    <li>Keep specificity low and predictable</li>\n                    <li>Start with a CSS reset or normalize</li>\n                    <li>Write component-based, reusable CSS</li>\n                    <li>Use utility classes for common adjustments</li>\n                    <li>Follow architecture patterns like ITCSS</li>\n                    <li>Optimize for performance</li>\n                    <li>Use CSS variables for design tokens</li>\n                    <li>Always consider maintainability and scalability</li>\n                </ul>\n            </section>\n        </div>\n        \n        <div class="lesson-navigation">\n            <a href="lesson11.html" class="btn-secondary">← Previous: CSS Variables & Functions</a>\n            <a href="../../index.html" class="btn-primary">Back to Dashboard →</a>\n        </div>\n    </main>\n    \n    <footer>\n        <p>&copy; 2024 Learner. Learn to code, one lesson at a time.</p>\n    </footer>\n</body>\n</html></create-file>\n</function_calls>'}
